                ConstructionDoneMsg=<color=255,240,100>Донесение из штаба:</color>
                ConstructionDoneMsg=Мы закончили сборку <color=255,240,100>транклюкатора</color>, босс. Новый механический друг с завидным нетерпением ожидает тебя на складе.
                Cost=-1
                CostCalc ^{
                    01=dword seed = Id(GetShipRuins(Player())) + CurTurn() * CurTurn();
                    02=int result_cost = max(Rnd(GalaxyMoney(2, 4) - 500, GalaxyMoney(2, 4) + 500, seed), 1000);
                    03=float TL_coef = -4.0 + GalaxyTechLevel();
                    04=if(TL_coef < 0) TL_coef = 0;
                    05=TL_coef = 0.5 * TL_coef + 1.0;
                    06=float Diff_coef = 0.85 + 0.15 * max(GalaxyDiffLevels(1) / 50 - 1, 1);
                    07=result_cost = round(TL_coef * Diff_coef * result_cost);
                    08=result_cost = result_cost + Rnd(-50, 100, seed);
                    09=if(result_cost <= 0) result_cost = 1;
                }
                DelayInProduction=365
                DelayInProductionAddText=[станет доступно через <NextProductionDaysLeft> дн.]
                Description=Проект: <clr>Транклюкатор<clrEnd>
                Description=Описание: Стандартный транклюкатор класса "Долбобот", какие в качестве автономной рабочей силы использовал ещё мой прадедушка. ActCodeBlocksList ^{
    ShuMercsHQ_GluonizingEnergy ^{
        00=[t_OnWeaponShot|]
        01=dword target = ScriptItemActObject1();
        02=if(ObjectType(target) > 5) exit;
        03=if(~ShipFindCustomShipInfoByType(target, 'ShuMercsHQ_GluonizationEffect'))
        03 ^{
            01=int effect_strength = ShipCustomShipInfoData(target, 'ShuMercsHQ_GluonizationEffect', 1) + 1;
            02=ScriptItemActParam(round((1.0 + min(0.10 * effect_strength, 6.5)) * ScriptItemActParam()));
            03=ShipCustomShipInfoData(target, 'ShuMercsHQ_GluonizationEffect', 1, effect_strength);
        }
        04=else
        04 ^{
            01=ShipAddCustomShipInfo(target, 'ShuMercsHQ_GluonizationEffect', 'NoShow', 1);
        }
    }
    ShuMercsHQ_GluonizingMissile ^{
        00=[t_OnMissileShot2|]
        01=dword target = ScriptItemActObject1();
        02=if(ObjectType(target) > 5) exit;
        03=if(~ShipFindCustomShipInfoByType(target, 'ShuMercsHQ_GluonizationEffect'))
        03 ^{
            01=int effect_strength = ShipCustomShipInfoData(target, 'ShuMercsHQ_GluonizationEffect', 1) + 1;
            02=dword missile = ScriptItemActObject2();
            03=MissileMinDamage(missile, round((1.0 + min(0.033 * effect_strength, 6.5)) * MissileMinDamage(missile)));
            04=MissileMaxDamage(missile, round((1.0 + min(0.033 * effect_strength, 6.5)) * MissileMaxDamage(missile)));
            05=ShipCustomShipInfoData(target, 'ShuMercsHQ_GluonizationEffect', 1, effect_strength);
        }
        04=else ShipAddCustomShipInfo(target, 'ShuMercsHQ_GluonizationEffect', 'NoShow', 1);
    }
    ShuMercsHQ_GluonizingSplinter ^{
        00=[t_OnWeaponShot|]
        01=dword target = ScriptItemActObject1();
        02=if(ObjectType(target) > 5) exit;
        03=if(~ShipFindCustomShipInfoByType(target, 'ShuMercsHQ_GluonizationEffect'))
        03 ^{
            01=int effect_strength = ShipCustomShipInfoData(target, 'ShuMercsHQ_GluonizationEffect', 1) + 1;

        }
        04=else
        04 ^{

        }

        01=dword cur_item = CurItem();
        02=ScriptItemData(cur_item, 1, ScriptItemData(cur_item, 1) - 1);
        03=if(!ScriptItemData(cur_item, 1))
        04 ^{
            01=int bon = FindBonusByNameInCfg('ShuMercsHQ_TetroazinePumping');
            02=ItemExtraSpecialsDeleteByType(cur_item, bon, ItemExtraSpecialsCountByType(cur_item, bon));

ShipInfo ^{
    AddInfo ^{
        CustomInfos ^{
            ChangeShipScriptGroupInfo ^{
                Description=NoShow
                Icon=0
                Name=Корабли с этой маркерной инфошкой будут автоматически переводиться в указанную скриптовую группу в тех скриптах, где для этого предусмотрены специальные проверки
            }
            DeadByHitInfo ^{
                Description=NoShow
                Icon=0
                Name=Корабли с этой маркерной инфошкой будут получать фатальный урон в случае попадания по ним корабля/оружия/предмета указанного в инфошке типа (можно вешать несколько инфошек сразу, если необходимо, чтобы цель погибала от нескольких разных типов урона)
                OnActCode ^{
                    01=dword cur_info = CurInfo();
                    02=dword cur_ship = ScriptItemActShip();
                    03=dword dealer = ScriptItemActObject1();
                    04=int obj_type = ObjectType(dealer);
                    05=if(obj_type != ShipCustomShipInfoData(0, cur_info, 1)) exit;
                    06=if(obj_type)
                    06 ^{
                        01=if(ShipCustomShipInfoData(0, cur_info, 2))
                        01 ^{
                            01=int num_type = 0;
                            02=if(obj_type == 4 || obj_type == 5) num_type = ShipTypeN(dealer);
                            03=else if(obj_type == 6) num_type = ItemType(dealer);
                            04=if(num_type != ShipCustomShipInfoData(0, cur_info, 2)) exit;
                        }
                        02=if(ShipCustomShipInfoData(0, cur_info, 3))
                        02 ^{
                            01=int obj_Id = 0;
                            02=if((obj_type >= 4 && obj_type <= 7) || obj_type == 1) obj_Id = Id(dealer);
                            03=if(obj_Id != ShipCustomShipInfoData(0, cur_info, 3)) exit;
                        }
                        03=str text_filt_1 = ShipCustomShipInfoTextData(0, cur_info, 1);
                        04=if(text_filt_1 != '')
                        04 ^{
                            01=str match_str = '';
                            02=if(obj_type == 6) match_str = EquipmentImageName(dealer);
                            03=if(match_str != text_filt_1) exit;
                        }
                    }
                    07=ScriptItemActParam(ScriptItemActParam() + HullHP(cur_ship));
                }
                OnActCodeTypes=t_OnTakingDamage,t_OnTakingDamageEn,t_OnTakingDamageSp,t_OnTakingDamageMi
            }
            IgnoreCamoInfo ^{
                Description=NoShow

            ShuMercsHQ_EMPTorpedoTargetHit ^{

            ShuMercsHQ_ExpirinStimulant ^{
                Description=Подставляется из раздела стимулятора.
                Icon=2
                Name=Экспирин
                OnActCode ^{
                    01=dword cur_info = CurInfo();
                    02=if(ScriptItemActionType(t_OnStep))
                    02 ^{
                        01=dword cur_ship = ScriptItemActShip();
                        02=int old_exp = ShipCustomShipInfoData(0, cur_info, 3);
                        03=int cur_exp = GetShipExpByType(cur_ship);
                        04=if(cur_exp > old_exp)
                        04 ^{
                            01=int new_exp = cur_exp - old_exp;
                            02=float percent = ShipCustomShipInfoTextData(0, cur_info, 2);
                            03=new_exp = round(percent * new_exp);
                            04=ShipFreeExp(cur_ship, ShipFreeExp(cur_ship) + new_exp);
                            05=SetShipExpByType(cur_ship, GetShipExpByType(cur_ship) + new_exp, 0);
                            06=ShipCustomShipInfoData(0, cur_info, 3, cur_exp);
                        }
                        05=int end_date = ShipCustomShipInfoData(0, cur_info, 1);
                        06=int artBioCheck = ArtefactTypeInUse(Player(), t_ArtBio);
                        07=if(artBioCheck)
                        07 ^{
                            01=if(RndObject(1, 100, cur_ship) <= 25 * artBioCheck) ShipCustomShipInfoData(0, cur_info, 1, end_date + 1);
                        }
                        08=if(end_date <= CurTurn())
                        08 ^{
                            01=str bons = ShipCustomShipInfoTextData(0, cur_info, 1);
                            02=for(int i = ParsCountFromString(bons, ',') - 1; i >= 0; i = i - 1)
                            02 ^{
                                01=str bon_str = GetParFromString(bons, ',', i, 0);
                                02=int bon = GetValueFromScript('', GetParFromString(bon_str, '=', 0, 0));
                                03=ShipSpecialBonuses(cur_ship, bon, ShipSpecialBonuses(cur_ship, bon) - GetParFromString(bon_str, '=', 1, 0));
                            }
                            03=ShipDeleteCustomShipInfo(cur_ship, 'ShuMercsHQ_ExpirinStimulant');
                            04=if(!ScriptItemActObject1()) Ether(0, '', Format(CT('Illness.Stimulant.Expirin.End'), '<Date'+'>', GameDateTxtByTurn(CurTurn()), '255,240,100'));
                        }
                    }
                    03=else
                    03 ^{
                        01=artBioCheck = ArtefactTypeInUse(Player(), t_ArtBio);
                        02=if(!artBioCheck)
                        02 ^{
                            01=if(ArtefactTypeInUse(Player(), t_ArtArtefactor))
                            01 ^{
                                01=for(i = ShipArts(Player()) - 1; i >= 0; i = i - 1)
                                01 ^{
                                    01=dword cur_art = ShipArts(Player(), i);
                                    02=if(ItemType(cur_art) == t_ArtBio)
                                    02 ^{
                                        01=if(ItemDurability(cur_art))
                                        01 ^{
                                            01=artBioCheck = 1;
                                            02=break;
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        03=if(!artBioCheck) ShipCustomShipInfoDescription(0, cur_info, ShipCustomShipInfoTextData(0, cur_info, 3));

                                            02 ^{
                                                01=if(perm) ItemDurability(cur_item, 100);

                                            03=else ItemDurability(cur_item, 100);
                                        }
                                        05=else ItemDurability(cur_item, 100);
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            08=if(perm)
                            09 ^{
                                01=for(j = 0; j < ShipArts(cur_ruin); j = j + 1)
                                02 ^{
                                    01=cur_item = ShipArts(cur_ruin, j);
                                    02=if(!ItemIsInUse(cur_item)) continue;
                                    03=if(ItemDurability(cur_item) < 100) ItemDurability(cur_item, 100);
                                }
                            }
                        }

                                        01=for(i = 1; i <= 5; i = i + 1)
                                        02 ^{
                                            01=if(ShipEqInSlot(cur_ship, t_Weapon1, i))
                                            02 ^{
                                                01=InterfaceText('Ship', 'GunBatteryLabelSlot' + i, 'x' + (attacks_count + 1));
                                                03=InterfaceState('Ship', 'GunBatteryLabelSlot' + i, 1);
                                            }
                                            03=else
                                            04 ^{
                                                01=InterfaceState('Ship', 'GunBatteryLabelSlot' + i, 0);
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                    04=else
                                    05 ^{
                                        01=for(i = 1; i <= 5; i = i + 1)
                                        02 ^{
                                            01=InterfaceState('Ship', 'GunBatteryLabelSlot' + i, 0);
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            12=else
                            13 ^{
                                01=for(i = 0; i < ShipItems(cur_ship); i = i + 1)
                                02 ^{
                                    01=item = ShipItems(cur_ship, i);
                                    02=cost = ItemExtraSpecialsCountByType(item, bon_num);
                                    03=if(!i)
                                    04 ^{
                                        01=NoDropItem(item, 1);
                                        02=if(cost)
                                        03 ^{
                                            01=ItemCost(item, cost);
                                            02=ItemExtraSpecialsDeleteByType(item, bon_num, cost);
                                        }
                                        04=continue;
                                    }
                                    05=if(!cost)
                                    06 ^{
                                        01=NoDropItem(item, 1);
                                        02=continue;
                                    }
                                    07=ItemCost(item, cost);
                                    08=ItemExtraSpecialsDeleteByType(item, bon_num, cost);
                                }
                                03=for(i = 0; i < ShipArts(cur_ship); i = i + 1)
                                04 ^{
                                    01=item = ShipArts(cur_ship, i);
                                    02=cost = ItemExtraSpecialsCountByType(item, bon_num);
                                    03=if(!cost)
                                    04 ^{
                                        01=NoDropItem(item, 1);
                                        02=continue;
                                    }
                                    05=ItemCost(item, cost);
                                    06=ItemExtraSpecialsDeleteByType(item, bon_num, cost);
                                }
                                05=if(~ShipFindCustomShipInfoByType(cur_ship, 'TrancNPCOwnerInfo'))
                                06 ^{
                                    08=item = CreateQuestItem('WeightReserve', 0);
                                    09=ItemSize(item, 0);
                                    10=AddItemToShip(cur_ship, item);
                                    11=NoDropItem(item, 1);
                                    12=ItemIsInUse(item, cur_ship, 1);
                                }
                                07=ArrangeItems(cur_ship);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                OnActCodeTypes=t_OnEnteringForm,t_OnReEnteringForm,t_OnLeavingForm,t_OnDeath
            }
        }
    }
